### 2.13.1.7 UL Receiver Characteristics Testing

#### 2.13.1.7.0-1 UL Receiver Characteristics Testing UL receiver characteristics testing (ID: 11211167)

**2.13.1.7.0-1.0-8**  (ID: `11211225`)

UL Receiver Characteristics Testing
UL receiver characteristics test is performed using pre-defined parameters for the requested PUSCH Fixed Reference Channel (FRC) as defined in chapter 7 of TS 38.141-1 and TS 38.141-2. The purpose of uplink Receiver testing is to verify PUSCH throughput, BER and BLER in different test cases. UL PUSCH signal is generated by signal generator. No HARQ retransmission needed.

[Before CNI-103796-A]

The supported FRCs and carrier BW are listed in below table.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| FRC | SCS | Supported Carrier BW (MHz) | Technology | Feature |
| G-FR1-A1-1 | 15kHz | 5, 10, 15, 20, 30, 35 | FDD | 5GC001037-B CB005881-B |
| G-FR1-A1-4 | 15kHz | 20, 25, 30, 35, 40, 50 | FDD | 5GC001037-B CB005881-B CB007201-C CB009222-A |
| G-FR1-A1-5 | 30kHz | 20, 30, 40, 50, 60, 70, 80, 90, 100 | FR1 TDD | 5GC001037-B FGCR-5027 5GC002493-C CB005881-B |
| G-FR1-A1-7 | 15kHz | 5 | FDD | 5GC001037-B |
| G-FR1-A2-1 | 15kHz | 5, 10, 15 | FDD |  |
| G-FR1-A2-4 | 15kHz | 20, 25, 30, 35, 40, 50 | FDD | 5GC001037-B CB005881-B CB007201-C CB009222-A |
| G-FR1-A2-5 | 30kHz | 20, 30, 40, 50, 60, 70, 80, 90, 100 | FR1 TDD | 5GC001037-B; FGCR-5027 5GC002493-C CB005881-B |
| G-FR2-A1-2 | 120kHz | 100 | FR2 TDD | 5GC001037-B |
| G-FR2-A1-3 | 120kHz | 100 | FR2 TDD | 5GC001037-B |
| G-FR1-A1-2 | 30kHz | 10,20, 30 | FR1 TDD | FGCR-5027 CB005881-B CB009500-A |
| G-FR1-A2-2 | 30kHz | 10 | FR1 TDD | CB009500-A |

[CNI-103796-A]

Refer to [5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] for detailled supported FRCs and carrier BW.

[End CNI-103796-A]

#### 2.13.1.7.0-2 UL Receiver Characteristics Testing Overview of 5G-L2-PS UL Process (ID: 11211234)

**2.13.1.7.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11211251`)

UL Receiver Characteristics Testing
[vsd\_desc]=== Diagram Content ===
IDLE
[Event triggers the slot based UL processing for next slot]
Slot Type Selection and
Beam Control
[otherwise]
[otherwise]
[UL processing end]
[5G-L2-PS test mode specific processing for UL]
[UL Transmission Slot in n+K2]
UL PUSCH Scheduling
=== Diagram Metadata ===
dc:creator: Chen, Hui 7. (Nokia - CN/Hangzhou)
Content-Type: application/vnd.visio[/vsd\_desc][vsd\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/attachments/m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file11103\_0.vsd[/vsd\_path]

After 5G-L2-PS receives receiver testing request from msg PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq for a specific cell, the cell enters UL receiver testing activated state.

For each cell in UL receiver testing activated state, 5G-L2-PS shall proceed with below slot level processing:

- The trigger to start the slot based processing of 5G-L2-PS for slot n is specified 5G\_L2\_455\_replaced([11152781](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24rCcvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The used subcarrier spacing is configured in PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq. Continue the below processing if the slot n+K2 is UL transmission slot. K2 = 2 used in test mode.

- The slot type selection and beam control for the UL transmission slots are specified in 5G\_L2\_1720\_replaced([11208427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-WMrfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_1723\_replaced([11208487](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-WzsfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- UL PUSCH scheduling in test mode is specified depending on uplink test type:

5G\_L2\_1769\_replaced([11211265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-evgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Receiver testing  [CB009222-B], FrcIndex is PUSCH Receiver listed in 5G\_L2\_1765\_replaced([11211167](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-eIc_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB009222-B] and receiverTestingConfig->harqEnable = False in msg PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq;

5G\_L2\_8785\_replaced([11211794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-hLyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Performance testing [CB009222-B] FrcIndex is PUSCH Performance listed in 5G\_L2\_1778\_replaced([11211482](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-f9ofvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB009222-B] and receiverTestingConfig->harqEnable = True [CB009222-B] or False [End CB009222-B] in msg PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.

When 5G-L2-PS receives PsTM\_StopConformanceTestReq to stop the receiver testing for a specific cell, the cell leaves UL receiver testing activated state. 5G-L2-PS shall stop the UL slot level processing of the cell. The stored measurement results shall be discarded.

Note: K2 is used in test mode to keep message timing in L2-L1 interface same as in normal case.

#### 2.13.1.7.1 UL PUSCH Transmission

##### 2.13.1.7.1.0-2 UL PUSCH Transmission UL PUSCH Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL in receiver testing (ID: 11211272)

**2.13.1.7.1.0-2.0-12**  (ID: `12723067`)

UL PUSCH Transmission
5G-L2-PS shall request the reception of an UL Transport Block by sending the message UlData\_PuschReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL. The IEs of channel parameter are filled according to the requested PUSCH Fixed Reference Channel (FRC).

Refer to [5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] for detailled configuration of each supported FRCs.

The IEs sfn and NR-Slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air.

IE tbSize\_bits: shall be set as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (UL, Transport Block Size Calculation) using LUT table according to the requested FRC type.

IE numOfPrb: set to Allocated resource blocks according to request FRC type.

IE modulationOrder: set to 2 for QPSK, 4 for 16QAM.

IE mcs: set to the mcs value according to requested FRC type.

IE rnti shall be set to 0.

IE cRnti: set to IE rnti.

IE numOfPuschSymbols shall be set to 14.

IE startSymbol shall be set to 0.

IE startPrb shall be equal to value of PRB\_Offset from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_610\_replaced([10978838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VWcXvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

IE antPort shall be set to **{0x8000} for rank 1 reception.**

IE spatialMode is set to "single antenna".

IE codebookIndex is set to 0.

IE puschTransCoherence is set to "fullCoherent".

IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt: **set to physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell\_CellSetupReq).**

IE nscId shall be set to 0.

IE ulPtrsFlag shall be set to false.

IEs ulPtrsTimeDensity, ulPtrsFrequencyDensity, ulPtrsResElemOffset are not used for PUSCH conformance receiver test. They are set to 0.

IE ulPtrsNumOfPorts is not used for PUSCH conformance receiver test, it is set to 1.

IE foeValid: set to true.

IE longTermCfoMetric: **refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3333\_replaced([11151157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

IE ulDmrsConfigType: set to 1.

IE ulDmrsLen: set to 1.

IE ulDmrsMappingType: set to typeA.

IE ulDmrsAddPos: set to 1.

IE numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData: Value 2 shall be used.

IE ulDmrsTypeAPos: set to "pos2".

The IEs [Before CB008949-A] baseGraph, numOfCodeBlocks, numOfFillerBits, liftSize,liftSizeSetIndex,codeBlockSize and liftSizeColumnIndex [CB008949-A] baseGraph (BG), numOfCodeBlocks (C), numOfFillerBits (F), liftSize (Z), liftSizeSetIndex (set\_index), codeBlockSize (K) and liftSizeColumnIndex [CB008949-A] shall be set as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (UL, Transport Block Size Calculation) using LUT table, The IE ncb and k0divZ are computed as described in 5G\_L2\_418 (RV = 0 is used).

IE rvIndex shall be set to 0.

IE numOfLayers shall be set to 1 Layer.

IE freshHarqTrans shall be set to true.

IE mcsTable shall be set to 64QAM.

IE harqProcessIndex: Indicates the harq process index of the selected HARQ process.

IE absoluteHarqProcessIndex shall be set as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5073\_replaced([11202321](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwcuQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE patternId: **[CB009514-I] if eCPRI 7.2e is enabled, set as described in 5G\_L2\_918 otherwise** [End CB009514-I] See 5G\_L2\_1723**.**\*\*\*\*

IE longTermCfoMetricOfAnt: refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3333\_replaced([11151157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE puschTransformPrecoderFlag: set to 0 for all PUSCH receiver FRCs.

IE ulPtrsNumOfGroups:set to 0.

IE ulPtrsNumOfSamplesPerGroup: **set to 0.**

IE ulRiSelectionThreshold**:** [Before CB009514-I] set to **rdUlRiSelectionThresh8Rx for** C8 subcellType else 0 **[CB009514-I] set according to** [End CB009514-I] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19768\_replaced([11140077](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**.*****\******\***

IE pBoost: set to cdmGroup without data (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19880\_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for **[Before CB013202-A]C8 subcellType** [CB013202-A] Pusch is 4Rx/8Rx/16Rx(numOfRxPusch=4/8/16, see 5G\_L2\_16925) **[End CB013202-A] else 0**.***\****\*

[CB010981-B]  
IE csi2EnhancedDetection = NRCELL.actPuschACSIPart2DtxEnhancement  
Refer to L1 requirement for details [11513756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_NV2wcPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) : 5G\_L1\_IF\_191  
[/CB010981-B]

For other IEs setting in this message, refer to related interface definition and the concerned features.

**Note:**

See the interface description for more details: **[Before CB009514-I] 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_183** [CB009514-I] 5G\_L1\_IF\_15538\_replaced([11513752](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy99vvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **[End CB009514-I] and following (procedure and message content) and** [Before CB009514-I] 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_293 **[CB009514-I] 5G\_L1\_IF\_15159\_replaced([11517633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSMmmfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** [End CB009514-I] (timing).***\******\***

##### 2.13.1.7.1.0-3 UL PUSCH Transmission UL PUSCH Receive Request L1 RU to 5G-L1-UL in receiver testing with eCPRI 7.2e enabled (ID: 11211372)

**2.13.1.7.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11211378`)

UL PUSCH Transmission
For each UL transmission slot, with eCPRI 7.2e enabled (actEcpri72e is true), UL scheduler shall send L1Data\_PuschReceiveReqL1ru in addition to L1Data\_PuschReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_812\_replaced([11204231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BggrQPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) instance handling the corresponding subcell to request the reception of PUSCH.

The IEs of PUSCH channel parameters are filled according to the requested PUSCH Fixed Reference Channel (FRC) defined in Annex A in TS 38.141-1/38.141-2.

Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed configuration for the supported PUSCH receiver test FRCs.

* IEs sfn and slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air.
* IE rnti: set to 0 (for single UE only).
* IE pairedUe: 0.
* IE fakeUe: set to false.
* IE numOfLayers: set to 1 Layer. Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE ulDmrsConfigType: set to 1.
* IE ulDmrsLen: set to 1.
* IE ulDmrsMappingType: set to Type A. Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE ulDmrsAddPos: set according to the requested FRC definition. Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE ulDmrsTypeAPos: set to "pos2".
* IE numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData: set to 2.
* IE nscId: set to 0 (for single UE only).
* IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt: set to physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell\_CellSetupReq).
* IE startPrb: set to the value of prbOffset from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_610\_replaced([10978838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VWcXvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* IE numOfPrb: set according to the requested FRC definition. Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE antPort: set to 0x8000 (if FRC is for 1 layer). Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE spatialMode: set to "single antenna".
* IE codebookIndex: set to 0.
* IE puschTransCoherence: set to fullCoherent.
* IE puschTransformPrecoderFlag: set according to the corresponding FRC definition. Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE foeValid: set to true.

**[Before CB014273-B]**

* IE longTermCfoMetricReal: set according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3333\_replaced([11151157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[End CB014273-B]**

* IE patternId: set patternId[0]=beamPatternIdList[0], patternId[1]=beamPatternIdList[1] from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq, patternId[2]=0, patternId[3]=0 (for numberofRxPusch=4). **[End CB014273-B]**

* IE numOfPrbExtra: set to 0 (for SU MIMO case), refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_14960\_replaced([11513820](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy-AvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_17838
* IE startAntIndex: set to 0 (for SU MIMO case), refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_14960\_replaced([11513820](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy-AvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**[Before CB014273-B]**

* IE ueReceiverSize: set to 4 (for numberOfrxBeamforming=4Rx), refer to 5G\_L2\_17840

**[CB014273-B]**

* IE ueReceiverSize: refer to 5G\_L2\_17840

**[End CB014273-B]**

**[Before CB014273-B]**

* IE suSplitpanelMode: ignored by 5G-L1-UL (for ueReceiverSize not equal to 16), and value 0 is filled with array size same as numOfBeams in patternId, refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_14960\_replaced([11513820](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy-AvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**[CB014273-B]**

* IE suSplitpanelMode: fill array of patternId size with 0 value

**[End CB014273-B]**

Note:

1. For other IEs setting in message L1Data\_PuschReceiveReqL1ru, refer to related L1 interface definition 5G\_L1\_IF\_14960\_replaced([11513820](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy-AvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (for message content), 5G\_L1\_IF\_15159\_replaced([11517633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSMmmfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message timing), and the concerned features;

##### 2.13.1.7.1.0-4 UL PUSCH Transmission Handling of PUSCH HARQ Feedback in receiver testing (ID: 11211386)

**2.13.1.7.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11211396`)

UL PUSCH Transmission
Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5082\_replaced([11203301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL HARQ handling, see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_293 and 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_294 for the possible msg timing. 5G-L2-PS shall store the measurement results as presented in below.

If UL CRC = OK:

tmMeasurementResult.numberOfReceivedBits += TBS size for the HARQ transmission.

tmMeasurementResult.numberOfReceivedTransmissionBlocks ++.

If UL CRC = NOK:

tmMeasurementResult.numberOfDefectiveTransmissionBlocks ++.

tmMeasurementResult.numberOfDefectiveBits += TBS size for the HARQ transmission.

If UL CRC = DTX:

tmMeasurementResult.numberOfUnreceivedTransmissionBlocks ++.

tmMeasurementResult.numberOfUnreceivedBits += TBS size for the HARQ transmission.

5G-L2-PS shall support control of the UL HARQ process aging, as in 5G\_L2\_430. When freeing a HARQ process due to HARQ aging, 5G-L2-PS shall update measurement results same as for HARQ failure:

tmMeasurementResult.numberOfUnreceivedTransmissionBlocks ++.

tmMeasurementResult.numberOfUnreceivedBits += TBS size for the HARQ transmission.

Note:

Measurement on defective and unreceived transmission is based on CRC result of each transmission. BLER can be calculated with the measurement results.

[CB008014-A]

For PUSCH performance test for UL timing adjustment with two UEs (one moving, one stationary), L2-PS shall update and report PUSCH measurement results for moving UE only.

[End CB008014-A]

---

##### 2.13.1.7.1.0-5 UL PUSCH Transmission Handling of PUSCH Receive Response from 5G-L1-UL in test mode (ID: 11211401)

**2.13.1.7.1.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11211419`)

UL PUSCH Transmission
5G-L2-PS shall handle the message UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs from 5G-L1-UL which has been triggered by the corresponding UlData\_PuschReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_190). See 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_293 and 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_294 for the possible msg timing.

5G-L2-PS shall store the RSSI measurement to measurement result:

tmMeasurementResult.rssi + = rssi;

tmMeasurementResult.rssiNumber ++.

5G-L2-PS shall record the measurement results from PuschUciBitsResp in message UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs from 5G-L1-UL

if CSI part 1 bits of UCI report equals predefined CSI part 1 pattern   tmMeasurementResult.detectedcounter1 += 1

else

tmMeasurementResult.missedcounter1 +=1

end if

if CSI part 2 bits of UCI report equals predefined CSI part 2 pattern    tmMeasurementResult.detectedcounter2 += 1

else

tmMeasurementResult.missedcounter2 +=1

end if

Note:

For test verification reference (calculated by tester)

CSI part 1 BLER = missedCounter1/(detectedCounter1 + missedCounter1)

CSI part 2 BLER = missedCounter2/(detectedCounter2 + missedCounter2)

[CB008014-A]

For PUSCH performance test for UL timing adjustment with two UEs (one moving, one stationary), L2-PS shall update and report PUSCH measurement results for moving UE only.

[End CB008014-A]

---

##### 2.13.1.7.1.0-6 UL PUSCH Transmission Handling of PUSCH measurement in test mode (ID: 11211425)

**2.13.1.7.1.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `11211454`)

UL PUSCH Transmission
5G-L2-PS shall report PUSCH measurement results to CP-RT in PUSCH\_report structure in PsTM\_MeasurementReportInd msg (5G\_L2\_IF\_619\_replaced([10979013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VXqe_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at the end of each measurement interval.

* IE rssi is the linear average of RSSIs measured during the measurement interval.
* IE numberOfReceivedBits shall be set to tmMeasurementResult.numberOfReceivedBits.
* IE numberOfDefectiveBits shall be set to tmMeasurementResult.numberOfDefectiveBits.
* IE numberOfUnreceivedBits shall be set to tmMeasurementResult.numberOfUnreceivedBits.
* IE numberOfReceivedTransmissionBlocks shall be set to tmMeasurementResult.numberOfReceivedTransmissionBlocks
* IE numberOfDefectiveTransmissionBlocks shall be set to tmMeasurementResult.numberOfDefectiveTransmissionBlocks.
* IE numberOfUnreceivedTransmissionBlocks shall be set to tmMeasurementResult.numberOfUnreceivedTransmissionBlocks.
* IE Throughput is calculated with below formula:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula defines "Throughput" as a fraction. The numerator is "numberOfReceivedBits × 100000000". The denominator is "numberOfReceivedBits + numberOfDefectiveBits + numberOfUnreceivedBits".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_11130.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB008014-A]

For PUSCH performance test for UL timing adjustment with two UEs (one moving, one stationary), L2-PS shall update and report PUSCH measurement results for moving UE only.

[End CB008014-A]

### 2.13.1.8 UL Performance Testing

###### 2.13.1.8.1 Supported PUSCH/PUCCH/PRACH performance test

###### 2.13.1.8.1-1 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-1.0-2**  (ID: `11211615`)

Supported PRACH performance test
L2-PS shall determine the performance testing type based on PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq with the rule as below:

* [Before CB009222-B]PUSCH performance test: type = Receiver and receiverTestingConfig-->harqEnable = True [CB009222-B]
* PUSCH performance test: type = Receiver and FrcIndex is PUSCH Performance described in 5G\_L2\_1778[End CB009222-B]
* PUCCH performance test: type = Control and controlChannelTestingConfig-->controlChanelTestType = PUCCH;
* PRACH performance test: type = Control and controlChannelTestingConfig-->controlChanelTestType = PRACH.

For performance test, the semistatic frame structure is defined in 5G\_L2\_2974. Performance testing for PUSCH, PUCCH or PRACH uses UL transmission slots.

The processing in 5G-L2-PS for PUSCH performance testing see 5G\_L2\_1766, 5G\_L2\_8785.

See 5G\_L2\_1785, 5G\_L2\_1794, 5G\_L2\_1802, 5G\_L2\_1804 for PUCCH performance testing.

5G\_L2\_1797, 5G\_L2\_1799 PUCCH format 1 and format 3 performance testing.

See 5G\_L2\_1785, 5G\_L2\_1786, 5G\_L2\_1789, 5G\_L2\_1801, 5G\_L2\_1803, 5G\_L2\_1805 for PRACH performance testing.

During the testing, 5G-L2-PS shall measure the performance for each cell in each measurement interval whose length is equal to reportingTimeInterval from msg PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_607\_replaced([10978822](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VWcW_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). 5G-L2-PS shall maintain a structure tmMeasurementResult to store the measurement results. tmMeasurementResult shall be reset to 0 at the start of each interval.

5G-L2-PS shall send the measurement results at the end of each measurement interval as specified in 5G\_L2\_1773 for PUSCH, 5G\_L2\_1804 for PUCCH, 5G\_L2\_1805 for PRACH.

When 5G-L2-PS receives PsTM\_StopConformanceTestReq to stop the testing for a specific cell, 5G-L2-PS shall stop the scheduling from next slot and the stored measurement results shall be discarded.

---

###### 2.13.1.8.1-2 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-2.0-2**  (ID: `13496008`)

Supported PRACH performance test
For PRACH performance test, L2-PS shall provide the PRACH transmission occasions list in cell setup response for FDD FR1 cells while flag actOranFDD in PsCell\_CellSetupReq is actived and PRACH format is 0 or 1.

The IEs of prachOccasions(see 5G\_L2\_IF\_161\_replaced([10967736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UUhkfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are filled according to the L2 interface 5G\_L2\_IF\_161\_replaced([10967736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UUhkfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) except following IEs:

-IE patternLength: set to 1. PRACH occasions repetition pattern length fixed to 10ms in conformance test. PRACH Configuration Period x fix to 1 and Offset y fix to 0 for all PRACH configuration indices.

-IE patternId: set absent. IE patternId used for performance test will be filled by 5G-CP-RT(see 5G\_L3\_IF\_1206).

-IE reOffsetMPlane: fix to 0 in conformance test.

-IE ceAxCIdList:  FDD [Before CB014950-B] only supports [End CB014950-B]  Non-Beamforming (Non-BF). So the ceAxCIdList size is 2 for subcellType(see 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))=A2, and 4 for subcellType(see 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))=A4.  [CB014950-B] For FDD Beamforming with ulSubcellType=A8, actPrachProbing=FALSE, ceAxCIdList is set as specified in [10967736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UUhkfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CB014950-B]

---

###### 2.13.1.8.1-3 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-3.0-4**  (ID: `11211692`)

Supported PRACH performance test
IE receivingSlot in PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_610\_replaced([10978838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VWcXvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) defines the receiving pattern for PUCCH and PRACH in gNB side. In TDD, the pattern repeats every 8 UL slots and only the 8 LSBs of receivingSlot are valid. In FDD, the pattern repeats every 10 UL slots and only the 10 LSBs of receivingSlot are valid. If  “1” is set for the corresponding UL slot, 5G-L2-PS shall consider PRACH or PUCCH is configured in the UL slot and shall indicate L1 to receive the PUCCH or PRACH as in 5G\_L2\_1794 for format 0 and format 2, 5G\_L2\_1797 for format 1 and 5G\_L2\_1799 for format 3 or 5G\_L2\_1801. Otherwise, L2-PS shall not indicate L1 to receive.

IE expectationSlot defines the transmission pattern of PUCCH or PRACH in test equipment (TE) side. In TDD, the pattern repeats every 8 UL slots and only the 8 LSBs of expectationSlot are valid. In FDD, the pattern repeats every 10 UL slots and only the 10 LSBs of expectationSlot are valid. If "1" is set for the corresponding UL slot, it's a transmission slot for TE to send PUCCH or PRACH; otherwise the slot is DTXed in TE side.

5G-L2-PS shall consider the two patterns start from the next frame boundary which meets below condition after the test request received in PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.

FR1 TDD: SFN modulo 2 = 0;

FR1 FDD: SFN modulo 1 = 0 (any frame boundary);

FR2: SFN modulo 2 = 0

The indicated slots for TE transmission in IE expectationSlot is a subset of the slots for gNB receiving as indicated in IE receivingSlot. 5G-L2-PS shall feedback PsTM\_StartConformanceTestResp with NOK in case of configuration error.

The slot which is marked as receiving slot in IE receivingSlot but not transmission slot in IE expectationSlot is referred to as "idle slot". For each idle slot, 5G-L2-PS shall count it in tmMeasurementResult during the measurement interval:

If the requested channel is PRACH or PUCCH format 2  or PUCCH format 3  with test type "UCI":

tmMeasurementResult.idlePeriodCounter =  tmMeasurementResult.idlePeriodCounter + 1

If the requested channel is PUCCH format 0 or 2  or format 1  with test type "ACK":

tmMeasurementResult.idlePeriodCounter =  tmMeasurementResult.idlePeriodCounter + nANPucch,

where nANPucch indicates number of ACK bits given in the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message, see 5G\_L2\_1794 for format 0&2, 5G\_L2\_1797 for format 1 and 5G\_L2\_1799 for format 3.

Mapping of bits in receivingSlot and expectationSlot to UL slots:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a sequence of colored squares, each containing a single letter. The squares are arranged horizontally. The colors and letters are as follows:

\* **Yellow squares with the letter 'S':** S, S, S
\* **Green squares with the letter 'U':** U, U, U, U, U

The squares are arranged horizontally and are evenly spaced.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_11163.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

The source file of the diagrams is available at: <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:u:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level/2%205G-L2-PS%20Component%20Requirements/2.12%20Testing/5G_L2_1785%20Bitmap%20for%20receivingSlot%20and%20expectationSlot.vsdx?d=w67162950cd36421391d2f416b86ce300&csf=1&web=1&e=Fvke9e>

[CB008474-C]

When PRACH scs is set to 15 kHz and PUSCH scs is set to 30 kHz in TDD FR1, it means one PRACH slot will need 2 bits to indicate. For format C2 with PRACH scs 15KHz/PUSCH scs 30kHz, one RACH occasion will occupy one 30kHz slot which means one bit of receivingSlot/expectationSlot.

Take supported PRACH config index 202 in CB008474-C for example, Subframe 9 is PRACH, for TDD configuration1 slot18 and slot19 are both UL slots and two bits indication needed here(slot18 LSB, slot19 MSB):

###### 2.13.1.8.1-4 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-4.0-3**  (ID: `11211739`)

Supported PRACH performance test
For PRACH performance test, the predefined delay offset pattern is supported if delayPatternSingleStepDuration > 0 is indicated in msg PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.

If delayPatternSingleStepDuration is bigger than 0, TE will send the preamble with a delay offset and the offset is increased within the loop, by adding in each step a value of 0.1us, until the end of the tested range, which is 0.9us for format 0 [PR687687] and format 1 [End PR687687]and 0.8us for other PRACH formats. Then the loop is being reset and starts from 0us again. See below figure. The duration for one delay step within one period is defined by delayPatternSingleStepDuration. The unit is slot. Only UL slot marked as transmission in expectationSlot (related bit = 1) is counted

L2PS detects PRACH format is 0 if prachConfigurationIndex of the msg PsCell\_CellSetupReq is below the value 28, else it is another PRACH format. Refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2005\_replaced([11275328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpGAOfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the relevant table of the 3GPP 38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2, 6.3.3.2-3 and 6.3.3.2-4.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays two diagrams illustrating delay offset patterns for different PRACH formats. Both diagrams show a series of boxes representing time intervals, labeled with delay offsets in microseconds (us). Above each series of boxes, a curved orange arrow indicates a progression or pattern.
The top diagram, labeled "Delay offset pattern for PRACH format 0 and format 1," shows delay offsets from 0us to 0.9us in increments of 0.1us. A bracket below the first few boxes points to "delayPatternSingleStepDuration."
The bottom diagram, labeled "Delay offset pattern for PRACH format A2, B4, C2," shows delay offsets from 0us to 0.8us in increments of 0.1us. Similar to the top diagram, a bracket below the first few boxes points to "delayPatternSingleStepDuration."
The overall presentation is a technical illustration, likely from a telecommunications or signal processing context, explaining how delay offsets are structured for different communication protocols.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_11167.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

If delayPatternSingleStepDuration is set to 0, 5G-L2-PS considers no delay offset pattern used in TE.

An example is shown as below:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a table with numerical data and a legend. The table has four rows and multiple columns. The first column contains text labels: "delay(us) for delayPatternSingleStepDuration=1", "delay(us) for delayPatternSingleStepDuration =2", "delay(us) for delayPatternSingleStepDuration =3", and "delay(us) for delay Pattern SingleStepDuration =4". The subsequent columns contain numerical values and "NA".
The legend below the table explains the color coding for different types of slots:
- Green: receiving slot
- Blue: expected slot
- Gray: other slot
The table itself appears to be a representation of delays in microseconds for different step durations, with different types of slots indicated by color in the header row (though the colors are not explicitly described in the OCR, they are visually present in the image).
Here is the table represented in markdown:

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| delay(us) for delayPatternSingleStepDuration =2 | NA | NA | 0 | NA | 0 | 0.1 | NA | 0.1 | 0.2 | NA | 0.2 | 0.3 | NA | 0.3 | 0.4 | NA | 0.4 |
| delay(us) for delayPatternSingleStepDuration =3 | NA | NA | 0 | NA | 0 | 0 | NA | 0 | 0.1 | NA | 0.1 | 0.2 | NA | 0.2 | 0.2 | NA | 0.3 |
| delay(us) for delay Pattern SingleStepDuration =4 | NA | NA | 0 | NA | 0 | 0 | NA | 0 | 0.1 | NA | 0.1 | 0.1 | NA | 0.3 | 0.3 | NA | 0.2 |

###### 2.13.1.8.1-5 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-5.0-3**  (ID: `11211787`)

Supported PRACH performance test
For PRACH performance test, if delaypatternsinglestepduration in PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq is greater than 0, 5G-L2-PS shall get delay offset pattern synchronized with test equipment as presented in below before sending PsTM\_StartConformanceTestResp; otherwise 5G-L2-PS feedbacks PsTM\_StartConformanceTestResp without the below operation. See delay offset pattern definition in 5G\_L2\_1786.

5G-L2-PS follows the below steps to find the starting of delay offset pattern:

1. In each PRACH transmission slot, i.e. the slot indicated by transmission pattern via IE expectationSlot (see 5G\_L2\_1785), 5G-L2-PS shall indicate L1 to receive PRACH by sending UlData\_PrachReceiveReq (see 5G\_L2\_1801).

2 If the preamble is detected correctly, i.e. expected preamble index is received, 5G-L2-PS estimates the delay offset for the slot:

delayOffset (i) = abs (preamble TA – constantOffset)

where preamble TA is the TA info received from L1 in UlData\_PrachReceiveInd; constantOffset is received in msg PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq; i is the index for each estimation, 5G-L2-PS shall record the SFN and Slot number for each estimation.

3. 5G-L2-PS calculates the averaged delay offset over the last nEst estimations, nEst = min(3, delaypatternsinglestepduration):

averagedDelayOffset(m) = [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is a fraction. The numerator is a summation symbol followed by "last nEst estimations delayOffset(i)". The denominator is "nEst".
$\sum\_{last\ nEst\ estimations} delayOffset(i) / nEst$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_11171.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

m is the index of averaged delay offset.

[Before PR672667] If abs(averagedDelayOffset(m) – averagedDelayOffset(m-1)) > rdPrachF0DelayJumpThreshold or rdPrachFxDelayJumpThreshold (see 5G\_L2\_1199, 5G\_L2\_1200) [PR672667]If  (averagedDelayOffset(m-1) – averagedDelayOffset(m)) > rdPrachF0DelayJumpThreshold or rdPrachFxDelayJumpThreshold (see 5G\_L2\_1199, 5G\_L2\_1200)  [End PR672667] depending on the requested PRACH format, 5G-L2-PS considers there is a delay offset jump from 0.9 or 0.8us to 0 us between the 2 slots which correspond to last 2 estimations and 5G-L2-PS considers the pattern starts from the slot corresponding to last estimation.

L2PS detects PRACH format is 0 if prachConfigurationIndex of the msg PsCell\_CellSetupReq is below the value 28, else it is another PRACH format. Refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2005\_replaced([11275328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpGAOfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the relevant table of the 3GPP 38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2, 6.3.3.2-3 and 6.3.3.2-4

Else 5G-L2-PS continues from step 1.

After 5G-L2-PS gets delay offset pattern synchronized with TE, L2-PS shall reply PsTM\_startConformanceTestResp with status = OK. 5G-L2-PS shall start normal PRACH receiving according to the receiving pattern, see 5G\_L2\_1785 and 5G\_L2\_1801, and start measurement, see 5G\_L2\_1803 and 5G\_L2\_1805.

If delay pattern can’t be found within time of rdSyncCounterThreshold(5G\_L2\_1201), L2 PS shall reply PsTM\_startConformanceTestResp with Nok and failure code is "sync\_failure".

Below example illustrates the calculation procedure assuming rdPrachF0DelayJumpThreshold = 0.2us, slot corresponding to i=6 is the slot starting from the beginning of delay offset pattern loop.

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a table with 4 rows and 8 columns. The first row contains column headers "i=0" through "i=7". The second row contains values for "delayOffset (i)" which are 0.8, 0.9, 0.9, 0.9, 0.9, 0.9, 0, and 0. The third row contains values for "m=0" through "m=5" under the corresponding "i" columns. The fourth row contains values for "averagedDelayOffset(m)" which are 0.867, 0.9, 0.9, 0.9, 0.6, and 0.3. The fifth row contains values for "Delta of averagedDelayOffset" which are 0.03, 0.00, 0.00, 0.00, 0.30, and an empty cell. An arrow points to the "0.30" value in the "Delta of averagedDelayOffset" row, with the text "Delay offset jump is found" below it.

|  | i=0 | i=1 | i=2 | i=3 | i=4 | i=5 | i=6 | i=7 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| delayOffset (i) | 0.8 | 0.9 | 0.9 | 0.9 | 0.9 | 0.9 | 0 | 0 |
|  |  |  | m=0 | m=1 | m=2 | m=3 | m=4 | m=5 |
| averagedDelayOffset(m) |  |  | 0.867 | 0.9 | 0.9 | 0.9 | 0.6 | 0.3 |
| Delta of averaged DelayOffset |  |  | 0.03 | 0.00 | 0.00 | 0.00 | 0.30 |  |

Note

The algorithm presented in the requirement assumes at least one PRACH transmission slot is configured in each step whose length is indicated by delayPatternSingleStepDuration.

---

###### 2.13.1.8.1-6 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-6.0-2**  (ID: `11211807`)

Supported PRACH performance test
For each UL transmission slot, a new transmission or retransmission shall be scheduled according to the requested PUSCH Fixed Reference Channel (FRC) type.

For a new transmission, 5G-L2-PS shall select the next available free HARQ process of the UE for the transmission of the TB. 5G-L2-PS shall provide an unused (free) absoluteHarqProcessIndex as defined in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1045. Note, the management of absoluteHarqProcessIndex is left to implementation. TBS and the used physical resource have been defined for each FRC in Annex A of TS 38.141-1/TS38.141-2.

[Before CB009222-B]

The maximum HARQ transmission number maxUlHarqTx = 4 is used in performance testing with fixed RV (Redundancy Version) sequence of 0, 2, 3, 1.

[CB009222-B]

If receiverTestingConfig->harqEnable = True

The maximum HARQ transmission number maxUlHarqTx = 4 is used in performance testing with fixed RV (Redundancy Version) sequence of 0, 2, 3, 1.

elseif receiverTestingConfig->harqEnable = False

The maximum HARQ transmission number maxUlHarqTx = 1 is used in performance testing with fixed RV (Redundancy Version) sequence of 0.

[End CB009222-B]

5G-L2-PS shall inform 5G-L1-UL about the PUSCH transmission as specified in 5G\_L2\_6247\_replaced([11211812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-hLy_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 5G-L2-PS shall store the TBS info for the selected HARQ process for measurement purpose.

5G-L2-PS shall handle PUSCH HARQ feedback as specified in 5G\_L2\_1771\_replaced([11211386](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-fWkfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall handle PUSCH Receive Response (UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs) as specified in 5G\_L2\_1772\_replaced([11211401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-fWlPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall discard the message of UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo.

---

###### 2.13.1.8.1-7 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-7.0-10**  (ID: `12723077`)

Supported PRACH performance test
For each UL transmission slot, UL scheduler shall send UlData\_PuschReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL instance handling the corresponding subcell to request the reception of PUSCH.

The IEs of channel parameter are filled according to the requested PUSCH Fixed Reference Channel (FRC) defined in Annex A in TS 38.141-1/38.141-2.

**[CB009514-I] Refer to 5G\_UP\_6643\_replaced([11367683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udjAh_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed configuration for the supported PUSCH performance test FRCs.** [End CB009514-I]\*\*\*\*

-IEs sfn and NR-Slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air.

-IE harqProcessIndex: Indicates the harq process index of the selected HARQ process.

-IE absoluteHarqProcessIndex shall be set such that the absoluteHarqProcessIndex values are assigned to HARQ processes uniquely within an L1 instance as described in 5G\_L2\_914\_replaced([11179261](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27FdQPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For PUSCH Performance test FRCs with two or more UEs, hint to keep test mode implementation simple and to ensure that absoluteHarqProcessIndex values are assigned uniquely among UEs is to split the range of absoluteHarqProcessIndex values [0,..,MAX\_HARQ\_CTX - 1] into non-overlapping sub-ranges, for example [0,..,19] for UE (rnti=0), [20,..,39] for UE (rnti=1), and so on.

-IE tbSize\_bits: shall be set as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (UL, Transport Block Size Calculation) using LUT table according to the corresponding FRC defined in chapter Annex A in TS 38.141-1 and 38.141-2.

* IE rnti: set to 0.

To meet 3GPP performance requirement for UL timing adjustment (TS 38.141-1 Section 8.2.5 and 38.141-2) to support two UEs, rnti :

set to 0 for moving UE, rnti : set to 1 for stationary UE.

- IE cRnti: set to IE rnti.

* IE ulDmrsConfigType: set to 1.
* IE ulDmrsLen: set to 1.
* IE ulDmrsMappingType: FR1: Type A or Type B, FR2: Type B. Set to typeA or typeB according to IE ulDmrsMappingType from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.
* IE ulDmrsAddPos: set according to the corresponding FRC defination in Annex A in 38.141-1 and 38.141-2. For FR1, only 1 needs to be supported; for FR2, {0 or 1} need to be supported.
* IE ulDmrsTypeAPos: set to "pos2".
* IE numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData: set to 2.
* IE startSymbol: set to 0.
* IE numOfPuschSymbols: FR1: 14, FR2: 10;
* IE startPrb: Set according to PRB offset in msg PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq. To support two UEs, startPrb is set according to (PRB offset in message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq) + Starting PRB index as defined in TS 38.141-1 Table 8.2.5.4.2-2 and 38.141-2, for the moving UE and stationary UE, respectively.
* IE numOfPrb: set according to the corresponding FRC defined in chapter Annex A in 38.141-1 and 38.141-2. Additionally, for the two UEs case, numOfPrb for each UE is set according to RB assignment defined in TS 38.141-1 Table 8.2.5.4.2-2 and 38.141-2.
* IEs mcs and modulationOrder are set according to the requested FRC type, refer to Annex A in TS 38.141-1 and 38.141-2 and summarized in below table. modulationOrder: set to 2 for QPSK, 4 for 16QAM, 6 for 64QAM, 8 for 256QAM.
* IE mcsTable: max64QAM or for FRCs with modulation=256QAM mcsTable is set to max256QAM.
* IE spatialMode: 2.
* IE codebookIndex: 0.
* IE nscId: 0. For the two UEs, nscID = 0 for moving UE, nscID = 1 for stationary UE as specified in 38.141-1 Table 8.2.5.4.2-2 and 38.141-2.

- IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt: set to physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell\_CellSetupReq).

* IE ulPtrsFlag: for FR1 set to 0; for FR2 set to TRUE or FALSE accoring to IE isPtrsFr2Enable from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq. **FALSE is expected for FRCs G-FR1-A3-31 and G-FR1-A3-32.**
* IE ulPtrsTimeDensity:FR1:NA; FR2: 1.
* IE ulPtrsFrequencyDensity:FR1: NA; FR2: 2.
* IE ulPtrsNumOfPorts: FR1:NA; FR2: set according to corresponding to requested FRC type, if the layer is 1, this IE is set to 1; if the layer is 2, this IE is set to 2; see below IE numOfLayers.
* IE ulPtrsResElemOffset:0.
* IE freshHarqTrans: set according to if it's the first transmission or retransmission.

- IE foeValid: set to true.

- IE longTermCfoMetric:

For FRC Index listed for HST:

G\_FR1\_A3\_34

G\_FR1\_A3\_34A

G\_FR1\_A4\_30

G\_FR1\_A4\_30A

refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3333\_replaced([11151157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* The IEs [Before CB008949-A] baseGraph, numOfCodeBlocks, numOfFillerBits, liftSize,liftSizeSetIndex,codeBlockSize and liftSizeColumnIndex [CB008949-A] baseGraph (BG), numOfCodeBlocks (C), numOfFillerBits (F), liftSize (Z), liftSizeSetIndex (set\_index), codeBlockSize (k) and liftSizeColumnIndex (column\_index) [End CB008949-A] shall be set as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (UL, Transport Block Size Calculation) using LUT table according to the requested FRC type. The IE ncb and k0divZ are computed as described in 5G\_L2\_418\_replaced([11152113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24mxA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE rvIndex: set according to RV pattern of 0, 2, 3, 1 for each HARQ transmission.
* IE numOfLayers: number of layers can be deduced from the time-frequency resource, modulation order and total number of bits per slot defined for the requested FRC. 1 and 2 layers are supported

For the value for each item please refer to the corresponding table in Annex A of TS 38.141-1 and 38.141-2.

* IE antPort: If the FRC is for one layer, set to 0x8000. If the FRC is for 2 layers, set to 0xC000.
* IE puschTransCoherence: set to fullCoherent.
* IE patternId: refer to 5G\_L2\_1723\_replaced([11208487](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-WzsfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

* IE puschTransformPrecoderFlag: set to 1 for FRCs G-FR1-A3-31 and G-FR1-A3-32, set to 0 for others.

- IE ulPtrsNumOfGroups: 0 for when transform precoder disabled, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5150\_replaced([11204236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwjb_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when transform precoder enabled.

- IE ulPtrsNumOfSamplesPerGroup: **0 for when transform precoder disabled, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5150\_replaced([11204236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwjb_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when transform precoder enabled.**

- IE PairedUe: 0.

###### 2.13.1.8.1-8 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-8.0-1**  (ID: `11211891`)

Supported PRACH performance test
For each UL transmission slot, with eCPRI 7.2e enabled (actEcpri72e is true), UL scheduler shall send message L1Data\_PuschReceiveReqL1ru in addition to L1Data\_PuschReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL (5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_812\_replaced([11204231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BggrQPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) instance handling the corresponding subcell to request the reception of PUSCH.

The IEs of PUSCH channel parameter are filled according to the requested PUSCH Fixed Reference Channel (FRC) defined in Annex A in TS 38.141-1/38.141-2. Refer to 5G\_UP\_6643\_replaced([11367683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udjAh_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed configuration for the supported PUSCH performance test FRCs.

* IEs sfn and slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air.
* IE rnti: set to 0 (for single UE only). To meet 3GPP performance requirement for UL timing adjustment (TS 38.141-1 Section 8.2.5 and 38.141-2) to support two UEs, rnti: set to 0 for moving UE, rnti : set to 1 for stationary UE.
* IE pairedUe: set to 0.
* IE fakeUe: set to false.
* IE numOfLayers: number of layer can be deduced from the time-frequency resource, modulation order and total number of bits per slot defined for the requested FRC. 1 and 2 layers are supported. For the value for each FRC, please refer to the corresponding table in Annex A of TS 38.141-1 and 38.141-2. Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE ulDmrsConfigType: set to 1.
* IE ulDmrsLen: set to 1.
* IE ulDmrsMappingType: set to typeA or typeB according to IE ulDmrsMappingType from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.
* IE ulDmrsAddPos: set according to the requested FRC definition in Annex A in 38.141-1 and 38.141-2. Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE ulDmrsTypeAPos: set to "pos2".
* IE numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData: set to 2.
* IE nscId: set to 0 (for single UE only). In case of two UEs, nscId = 0 for moving UE, nscId = 1 for stationary UE as specified in 38.141-1 Table 8.2.5.4.2-2 and 38.141-2.
* IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt: set to physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell\_CellSetupReq).
* IE startPrb: set according to PRB offset in msg PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq. To support two UEs, startPrb is set according to (PRB offset in message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq) + Starting PRB index as defined in TS 38.141-1 Table 8.2.5.4.2-2 and 38.141-2, for the moving UE and stationary UE, respectively.
* IE numOfPrb: set according to the requested FRC defined in chapter Annex A in 38.141-1 and 38.141-2. Additionally, for the two UEs case, numOfPrb for each UE is set according to RB assignment defined in TS 38.141-1 Table 8.2.5.4.2-2 and 38.141-2. Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* IE antPort: If the FRC is for one layer, set to 0x8000. If the FRC is for 2 layers, set to 0xC000.
* IE spatialMode: set to 2.
* IE codebookIndex: set to 0.
* IE puschTransCoherence: set to fullCoherent.
* IE puschTransformPrecoderFlag: set according to requested FRC (1 for FRCs G-FR1-A3-31 and G-FR1-A3-32, set to 0 for others). Refer to 5G\_UP\_12312\_replaced([11367583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udiZdvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1. For other IEs setting in message L1Data\_PuschReceiveReqL1ru, refer to related L1 interface definition 5G\_L1\_IF\_14960\_replaced([11513820](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy-AvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message content), 5G\_L1\_IF\_15159\_replaced([11517633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSMmmfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message timing), and the concerned features.

---

###### 2.13.1.8.1-9 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-9.0-1**  (ID: `11211904`)

Supported PRACH performance test
On receiving PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq message to start PUSCH performance test for UL timing adjustment, L2-PS (PsTm) shall enter TA\_MONITORING\_STATE for the moving UE (it is left to implementation to decide how the state is represented internally in conformance test mode)

* On entering TA\_MONITORING\_STATE for the moving UE, L2-PS shall perform the following:

a. Initialize rrmUePuschLongTermTimingOffset[ue,t] to INVALID value.

b. Initialize TAC to the neutral value (31).

c. Start 'TAC calculation period' timer with periodicity as per configured rdTacPeriodicityMs value.

* When ((L2-PS is in TA\_MONITORING\_STATE for the moving UE) AND ('TAC calculation period' timer is still active))

L2-PS shall send UlData\_PuschReceiveReq message to L1-UL with IE taMacCeValueTM set to the neutral  value (31) for the moving UE.

* On reception of UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs message from L1-UL, L2-PS shall perform the following:

if ((dtx reported for the moving UE is nonDTX) AND (shortTermTaMetric reported for the moving UE is valid as defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_201\_replaced([11513837](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND (shortTermTaPeakAmp for moving UE is > 0 as defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_201\_replaced([11513837](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) then

Calculate rrmUePuschLongTermTimingOffset[ue,t] as per formula defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3312\_replaced([11150143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksR__fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with puschShortTermTimingOffset[ue] set to IE shortTermTaMetric value for the moving UE received in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs message.

* On expiry of 'TAC calculation period' timer, L2-PS shall peform the following for the moving UE:

Calculate TAC as per formula defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3317\_replaced([11150271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksSnDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with rrmUeLongTermTimingOffset set to current rrmUePuschLongTermTimingOffset[ue, t]

Check if the calculated TAC value needs to be sent to L1-UL as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3319\_replaced([11150376](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksTOFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

if  ((TAC is not equal to 31) AND abs(rrmUeLongTermTimingOffset) >=  rdTacEmitPreventThreshold)) then

Clip the calculated TAC value within range [31 - rdTacMinStep ; 31 + rdTacMaxStep].

Set IE taMacCeValueTM to clipped TAC value.

else

Set IE taMacCeValueTM to neutral TAC value (31).

Send UlData\_PuschReceiveReq message with IE taMacCeValueTM set for the moving UE to L1-UL.

On sending the UlData\_PuschReceiveReq message with TAC value for the moving UE, L2-PS shall perform the following:

a. Reset rrmUePuschLongTermTimingOffset[ue,t] to INVALID value.

b. Reset TAC to neutral value (31).

c. Restart 'TAC calculation period' timer with periodicity (rdTacPeriodicityMs).

* On receiving PsTM\_StopConformanceTestReq to stop PUSCH performance test for UL timing adjustment, L2-PS (PsTm) shall exit TA\_MONITORING\_STATE for the moving UE.

---

###### 2.13.1.8.1-10 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1-10.0-4**  (ID: `11211934`)

Supported PRACH performance test
5G-L2-PS shall send UlData\_PUCCHReceiveReq to L1 for the UL slot which is indicated as receiving slot in the receiving pattern as defined in 5G\_L2\_1785\_replaced([11211631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-gkwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The msg content and transmission timing of UlData\_PucchReceiveReq see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_211 and 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_273.

5G-L2-PS shall set the value to each IEs in UlData\_PUCCHReceiveReq as in below:

IE numOfPucchResources : set to 1.

IE rnti: set to 0.

IE pucchFormat: set to 0 or 2 according to received PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.

IE numOfLayers: set to 1.

IE numOfAntennaPorts: set to 1.

IE harqProcessIndex: set to 0.

IE startPrb: set to prbOffset under structure pucch in PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.

IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt: set to physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell\_CellSetupReq).

IE dataScramblingInt: set to physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell\_CellSetupReq).

IE srBitDetection: set to false for PUCCH format 0; set to invalid for PUCCH format 2.

Below IEs are set according to requested PUCCH format and test type in msg:

PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq. numPucchSymbol in PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq is used to indicate ACK or UCI test for format 2, 1 symbol for ACK and 2 symbols for UCI.

IE numOfPrb:

- PUCCH format 0: 1;

- PUCCH format 2 for ACK: 4;

- PUCCH format 2 for UCI: 9.

IE nANPucch: set to numPayloadBit in PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq for ACK/NACK test, set to 0 for UCI Bler test.

IE numOfBitsOfUciInformation: Set to numPayloadBit in PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.

IE numOfSymbols: Set to numPucchSymbol in PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.

IE firstSymbol: set to 13 if IE numOfSymbols = 1; set to 12 if IE numOfSymbols = 2.

IE frequencyHopping: set to enabled if numOfSymbols = 2; disabled if numOfSymbols = 1.

IE secondHopPrb: largestPrbIndex – (numOfPrb – 1), where largestPrbIndex from PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq.

IE initialCyclicShift: set to 0.

IE patternId: Refer to 5G\_L2\_1723\_replaced([11208487](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-WzsfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IE longTermCfoMetric:

[Before PR638903]

real and imaginary parts are equal to 1.0 and 0.0 respectively.

[PR638903]

refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3333\_replaced([11151157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End PR638903]

IE longTermCfoMetricOfAnt:

[Before PR638903]

longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0]: 1+0j

longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1]: 1+0j

longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[2]: 1+0j for A4/C4 UL subcell or INVALID(0+0j) for A2/C2/D2 UL subcell

longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[3]: 1+0j for A4/C4 UL subcell or INVALID(0+0j) for A2/C2/D2 UL subcell.

[PR638903]

refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3333\_replaced([11151157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End PR638903]

IE timeDomainOcc: set to 0

Note: For other IEs setting in this message, refer to 5G\_L2\_945\_replaced([11180313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Lj7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PUCCH format 0 and 5G\_L2\_952\_replaced([11180418](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27MK__vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PUCCH format 2.

---

###### 2.13.1.8.1-13 Supported PRACH performance test

###### 2.13.1.8.1-14 Supported PRACH performance test

###### 2.13.1.8.1-15 Supported PRACH performance test

###### 2.13.1.8.1-16 Supported PRACH performance test

###### 2.13.1.8.1-17 Supported PRACH performance test

**2.13.1.8.1.0-1**  (ID: `11211469`)

Supported PUSCH/PUCCH/PRACH performance test
General

The purpose of UL performance test is to verify the BTS performance defined in chapter 8 of TS 38.141-1 and TS 38.141-2. Performance test includes the PUSCH performance test, PUCCH performance test and PRACH performance test.

For PUSCH performance test, the supported FRCs are defined 5G\_L2\_1777;

For PUCCH performance test, the supported formats are defined 5G\_L2\_1780;

For PRACH performance test, the supported formats are defined 5G\_L2\_1782;

### 2.13.1.9 Common IEs setting from L2-PS to L1-UL and L1-DL

#### 2.13.1.9.0-1 Common IEs setting from L2-PS to L1-UL and L1-DL IEs in structure eCpriConfig setting for PUCCH/PUSCH (ID: 11212041)

**2.13.1.9.0-1.0-8**  (ID: `13428446`)

Common IEs setting from L2-PS to L1-UL and L1-DL
PUSCH/PUCCH: The following is followed for setting the structure eCpriConfig (5G\_L1\_IF\_266\_replaced ([11514645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dj_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), in UlData\_PuschReceiveReq and UlData\_PucchReceiveReq for eCPRI configuration purpose.

Note:

With eCPRI 7.2e enabled, for the filling of IE patternId in L1Data\_PuschReceiveReqL1ru, refer to 5G\_L2\_23778\_replaced([11211372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-evjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (PUSCH receiver test), 5G\_L2\_23715\_replaced([11211885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-hy1vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (PUSCH performance test)

5G-L2-PS shall populate fields in structure eCpriConfig in UlData\_PuschReceiveReq, UlData\_PucchReceiveReq messages based on eCpriFlag.

If eCpriFlag = true :

-numCeAxCIndex: set according to ulSubcellType from PsCell\_CellSetupReq. Set to:

8 if subcellType is C8 [CB014950-B] or A8 [End CB014950-B]

4 if subcellType is A4 or C4

otherwise set to 2

**-ceAxCIndex: (0,1) if numCeAxCIndex is 2**

(0,..,3) if numCeAxCIndex is 4

(0,..,7) if numCeAxCIndex is 8

-patternId[4]:

For PUSCH test if ulSubcellType is C8 and activeBeamforming is true:

[CB014950-B]For PUSCH test if (ulSubcellType is A8) and (activeBeamforming is true) and (numberofRxBeamforming=8): [End CB014950-B]

For PUCCH test if ulSubcellType is C8 [CB014950-B] or A8, [End CB014950-B] and activeBeamforming is true and numberOfRxPucch=8:

patternId[0]=beamPatternIdList[0] and patternId[1]=beamPatternIdList[1], patternId[2]=beamPatternIdList[2] and patternId[3]=beamPatternIdList[3].

For PUSCH/PUCCH test if ulSubcellType is C4 and activeBeamforming is true:

For PUCCH test if ulSubcellType is C8 and activeBeamforming is true and numberOfRxPucch=4:

patternId[0]=beamPatternIdList[0] and patternId[1]=beamPatternIdList[1], patternId[2]=0 and patternId[3]=0.

For other configurations:

patternId[0]=beamPatternIdList[0] and patternId[1]=beamPatternIdList[0], patternId[2]=0 and patternId[3]=0.

If eCpriFlag = False :

5G-L2-PS shall populate fields in structure eCpriConfig in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, UlData\_PuschReceiveReq messages (as per 5G\_L1\_IF\_266\_replaced([11514645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dj_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))).

- numCeAxCindex: set to value 4

- eAxCIndex: set to value (0, 0, 0, 0)

- patternId[4]: elements are set to 0

5G-L2-PS shall populate fields in structure staticLongPucchConfigEcpri in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, messages based on eCpriFlag.

If eCpriFlag = true :

* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerDedicated.startPrb to value from field prbOffset under structure pucch in PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_610\_replaced([10978838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VWcXvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerDedicated.numPrb to value according to 5G\_L2\_1794\_replaced([11211909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-hy2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerDedicated.eCpriSectionId set to value describe below
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperDedicated.numPrb to value according to 5G\_L2\_1794\_replaced([11211909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-hy2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperDedicated.startPrb set to( largestPrbIndex (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_610\_replaced([10978838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VWcXvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  + 1 - eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperDedicated.numPrb)
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperDedicated.eCpriSectionId set to value describe below
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerCommon.startPrb = 0
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerCommon.numPrb = 0
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerCommon.eCpriSectionId set to value describe below
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperCommon.startPrb = 0
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperCommon.numPrb = 0
* eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperCommon.eCpriSectionId set to value describe below
* startSymbol set as firstSymbol according to 5G\_L2\_1794\_replaced([11211909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-hy2vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numSymbols se to value from numPucchSymbol (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_610\_replaced([10978838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VWcXvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

End

-eCpriSectionId in PUCCH and PUSCH:

If **eCpriFlag is true and FD beamforming is enabled (ulEcpriFdBeamforming = True):**

For PUCCH, both eCpriSectionID[0] and eCpriSectionID[1] are set to 0.

For PUSCH, eCpriSectionID is set to 0.

Otherwise, fill all bits with '1'.

if (actEcpri72e=true) and (eCpriFlag = true) and (activeBeamforming is true)

For PUSCH test: IEs in UlData\_PuschReceiveReq

- structure eCpriConfig: Refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_610\_replaced([10978838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VWcXvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_L2\_IF\_5511\_replaced([10979038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VYRgfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_L1\_IF\_191\_replaced([11513756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy99_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_L2\_918\_replaced([11179293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27FdRvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For PUCCH test: IEs in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq

- structure eCpriConfig: Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_15541\_replaced([11514123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aOPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- numCeAxCindex: set to numOfRxPucch (Refer 5G\_L2\_16925\_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- patternId: depends on numberofRxPucch, set patternId[0 … (numberofRxPucch/2)-1]=beamPatternIdList[0 … (numberofRxPucch/2)-1] from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq or PsTM\_BeamPatternChangeReq, if remaining unset patternId they should be set to 0.

end  (actEcpri72e=true)

refer to 5G\_L2\_13602\_replaced([11212090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-jA-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PRACH;

#### 2.13.1.9.0-2 Common IEs setting from L2-PS to L1-UL and L1-DL IEs in structure eCpriConfig setting for PRACH (ID: 11212090)

**2.13.1.9.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11212108`)

Common IEs setting from L2-PS to L1-UL and L1-DL
PRACH: The following is followed for setting the structure eCpriConfig(5G\_L1\_IF\_266\_replaced([11514653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dkfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in UlData\_PrachReceiveReq for eCPRI configuration purpose:

**[Before CB009514-I]**

eCpriFlag = true

**[CB009514-I]**

eCpriFlag = true and actEcpri72e= false

**[End CB009514-I]**

5G-L2-PS shall use the highest two or the highest four ceAxCIndex choices for UlData\_PrachReceiveReq according to numCeAxCId  in ulSubcellList structure from PsCell\_CellSetupReq

-numCeAxcIndex:  set to 4 if numCeAxCId is 8 or 12, set to 2 for others .

-ceAxcIndex: (numCeAxCId-2, numCeAxCId-1) or (numCeAxCId-4, numCeAxCId-3,numCeAxCId-2, numCeAxCId-1) if numCeAxcIndex is 2 or 4 respectively;

-patternId[4]: elements are set to beamPatternId from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq or PsTm\_BeamPatternChangeReq;

**[CB009514-I]**

eCpriFlag = true and actEcpri72e= true

-numCeAxcIndex:  set to 4 **[CB014273-B] (whatever ulSubCellType Cx\_y)**[End CB014273-B]\*\*\*\*

-5G-L2-PS shall use numberOfRXPucch as starting index and numCeAxcIndex as the array size from ulSubcellList structure in PsCell\_CellSetupReq to retrieve PRACH ceAxcIndex list.

PRACH ceAxcIndex list is used to filll ecpriConfig ceAxcIndex elements in UlData\_PrachReceiveReq (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_15392\_replaced([11514303](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oWfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and prachOccasions ceAxCIdList elements in PsCell\_CellSetupResp(refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_161\_replaced([10967736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UUhkfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

-ceAxcIndex list: (numberOfRxPucch, numberOfRxPucch+1, numberOfRxPucch+2, numberOfRxPucch+3)

-patternId[2]: elements are set to beamPatternId from 2 first elements of message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq or PsTm\_BeamPatternChangeReq;

**[End CB009514-I]**

eCpriFlag = false

When eCpriFlag is false, 5G-L2-PS sets two ceAxCIndex choices (0, 0) and patternIds to value 0  in the UlData\_PrachReceiveReq.

#### 2.13.1.9.0-3 Common IEs setting from L2-PS to L1-UL and L1-DL IEs in structure eCpriConfig/streamConfig setting for PDSCH/PDCCH (ID: 11212116)

**2.13.1.9.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13365641`)

Common IEs setting from L2-PS to L1-UL and L1-DL
PDSCH/PDCCH: The following is followed for setting the structure StreamConfig (5G\_L1\_IF\_15591\_replaced([11512962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteY_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and eCpriConfig (5G\_L1\_IF\_110\_replaced([11512672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrCMvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DlData\_PdschSendReq and DlData\_PdcchSendReq, respectively, for eCPRI configuration purpose:

5G-L2-PS shall populate fields in structure eCpriConfig in DLData\_PdcchSendReq message:

- numCeAxCindex: set according to dlMimoMode, dlSubcellType from PsCell\_CellSetupReq message. Set to 1 if dlSubcellType is A1 and dlMimoMode is "SingleAntennaTransmission\_1x1". Set to 4 if dlSubcellType is A4 or C4 and dlMimoMode is 4x4 or 4x2, otherwise set to 2.

[CB008577-D]

For FDD BF , with dlMimoMode is 32\*4 , numCeAxCindex will be set to 2,  according PDCCH's precoding supported by [11095854: PDCCH transmission for conformance test only](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmpSBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[End CB008577-D]

- ceAxCIndex: set to {0} or {0,1} or {0,1,2,3} if numCeAxCindex is 1 or 2 or 4, respectively.

- patternId[2]: if dlSubcellType is A1 and dlMimoMode is "SingleAntennaTransmission\_1x1" both elements are set to zero otherwise both elements are set to elements in beamPatternIdList from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq or PsTm\_BeamPatternChangeReq.

Structure streamConfig for PDSCH for both CPRI and eCPRI:

- numStreamIndex: set according to dlMimoMode/dlSubcellType from PsCell\_CellSetupReq for DL;

Set to 1 if dlSubcellType is A1 and dlMimoMode is "SingleAntennaTransmission\_1x1" (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_34\_replaced([11512305](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRol4fvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))); Set to 4 if subcellType is A4 or C4 and MIMO mode is 4x4, otherwise set to 2.

[CB008577-D]

For FDD BF , with dlMimoMode is 32\*4, numStreamIndex shall be set according to PDSCH's precoding with 32 port CSI-RS（[11097098: Precoding for conformance test only](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km04N_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

Informative note: The precoding parameters are from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq as legacy dlmimomode 4x4, it is CB014950's responsibility to extend the  codebook setting to support all 32 port CSI-RS.

[End CB008577-D]

- streamIndex: (0) or (0,1) or (0,1,2,3) if numStreamIndex is 1 or 2 or 4 respectively.

- patternId[2]: if dlSubcellType is A1 and dlMimoMode is "SingleAntennaTransmission\_1x1" both elements are set to zero otherwise both elements are set to elements in beamPatternIdList from message PsTM\_StartConformanceTestReq or PsTm\_BeamPatternChangeReq.

Note: For the older versions of this requirement (filling eCPRI/StreamConfig for PDCCH and PDSCH) please refer to 5G\_L2\_1807\_replaced([11212041](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-jA8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 2.13.1.9.0-4 Common IEs setting from L2-PS to L1-UL and L1-DL IE bufferedUlConfig setting for PUSCH and PUCCH channels (ID: 11212125)

**2.13.1.9.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11212132`)

Common IEs setting from L2-PS to L1-UL and L1-DL
Requesting Transport Block receiving from 5G-L1-UL about IE bufferedUlConfig setting for PUSCH and PUCCH channels

For structure bufferedUlConfig(5G\_L1\_5G21A\_264) in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq/UlData\_PuschReceiveReq messages:

5G-L2-PS shall assume that Buffered UL is used when bufferedUlAllowed  is True in PsCnfg\_AddressDistributionReq (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_8\_replaced([10966028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UL-sfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))); If Buffered UL is used in conformance test, 5G-L2-PS shall shall set processInRealTime  as False or True  based on L1 process capacity. the “L1 capability for the number of subcells per L1 instance” shall NOT be exceeded when allocating RT UL subcells as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5209\_replaced([11209950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw2W9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

5G\_L2-PS shall have the following variables to control number of RT subcells for each subcell type:

maxNumOfC2RtUlSubcell = 2;

maxNumOfC4RtUlSubcell = 1;

maxNumOfD2RtUlSubcell = 2;

If processInRealTime is set to True, then slotForProcessing and sfnForProcessing are set to the same values as slot and sfn from given message.

If processInRealTime is set to False, then slotForProcessing and sfnForProcessing are set to the slot and SFN selected for delayed (non-real time) processing.

To select for delayed (non-real time) processing SFN and slot, fixed time slot delay is used according to frame structure(5G\_L2\_2974\_replaced([11208435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-WMrvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))); 3/2/5 slots delay for below frame structures accordingly:

Configuration1: 7D1S2U, S=6D:4G:4U;

Configuration2: 3D1S1U, S=10D:2G:2U;

Configuration3: 3D1S4U2D, S=6D:4G:4U;

Note: Conformance test is running in one subcell per cell even with multiple subcells per cell.

Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5192\_replaced([11209845](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw2W4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more details about Buffered UL.

## 2.13.2 Artificial Load

### 2.13.2.0-2 Artificial Load General principles of artificial PDSCH load for DL performance testing (ID: 11212150)

**2.13.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11212162`)

Artificial Load
When [Before CNI-116869] targetTotalLoad [CNI-116869] totalLoad [End CNI-116869] of artificialLoadInfo included in PsCell\_CellSetupReq or PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq is larger than 0, it means artificial PDSCH load needs to be generated in this cell. L2-PS does not need to create UE context for the artificial load. One special C-RNTI needs to be reserved for the dummy user, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3391\_replaced([11151993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksc_HPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Control plane does not need to be informed about this C-RNTI.

Artificial load is created only on PDSCH; no other channels or signals are affected.

---

### 2.13.2.0-4 Artificial Load Scheduler actions for reconfiguration of the artificial PDSCH load for DL performance testing (ID: 11212173)

**2.13.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11212187`)

Artificial Load
The artificial load can be controlled online by the cell reconfiguration procedure.

1. When [Before CNI-116869] targetTotalLoad [CNI-116869] totalLoad [End CNI-116869] of artificialLoadInfo changes from zero to a non-zero value during PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq message procedure, artificial PDSCH load needs to be generated.
2. When [Before CNI-116869] targetTotalLoad [CNI-116869] totalLoad [End CNI-116869] of artificialLoadInfo changes from a non-zero value to zero during PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq procedure, the artificial load generation needs to be deactivated.
3. When [Before CNI-116869] targetTotalLoad [CNI-116869] totalLoad [End CNI-116869] of artificialLoadInfo is a non-zero value before and after PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq procedure, new artificialLoadInfo parameters (load, MCS, beam) need to be taken into account.

---

### 2.13.2.0-5 Artificial Load PDSCH request for artificial load (ID: 11212192)

**2.13.2.0-5.0-8**  (ID: `13347117`)

Artificial Load
In the slots where artificial PDSCH load needs to be created (according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4104\_replaced([11183791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvNYI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17426\_replaced([11183931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ), 5G-L2-PS shall request L1-DL to create the artificial load by sending message *DlData\_PdschSendReq to 5G-L1-DL. General content of the message is defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_87\_replaced([11512751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Below we define parameter values that are specific for the artificial load and are not present in other requirements. Values that are not present below, nor in other requirement for the artificial load, follow the normal procedure defined in 5G\_L2\_887\_replaced([11178401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26_9tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

For the artificial load, the values below shall be used:

* dmrsScramblingSequenceInt: fixed to 0
* nscId: fixed to 0
* spatialMode: as determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3196\_replaced([11184070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvP0Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* PdschPrecodingConfig: as determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3196\_replaced([11184070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvP0Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* startPrb: As determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4510\_replaced([11181328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-Hn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numOfPrb:  As determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4510\_replaced([11181328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-Hn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* when actRat1Alloc set as false, then use rat0Bitmap: As determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4510\_replaced([11181328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-Hn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* subcellId: ID of unused L1 DL subcell (if multiple are available, choose the one with smallest ID)
* PTRS parameters: as determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4670\_replaced([11192667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZs_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numOfLayers: for rank selection see:
* For artificial PDSCH load for DL performance testing: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3193\_replaced([11183902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_O_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* For DL artificial load generation over sector beam and for DL artificial load generation for EMF validation: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17426\_replaced([11183931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* tbsLbrm shall be selected according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4663\_replaced([11192576](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlyovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) based on the following inputs
* No 256QAM
* The allocated **FD Resourceas determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4510\_replaced([11181328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-Hn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**
* Maximum number of layers supported by the cell, as given by dlMimoMode in *PsCell\_CellSetupReq: 2 layers for 2x2 MIMO modes , 4 layers for 4x4 MIMO modes And CL 8x4* *MIMO mode[CB008577-D] and CL 32x4 MIMO mode[End CB008577-D].*\*\*
* modulationOrder and rest of the channel encoding parameters (baseGraph (BG), numOfCodeBlocks (C), codeBlockSize (K), numOfFillerBits (F), liftSize (Z), liftSizeSetIndex (set\_index) ) shall be set based on mcsIndex defined in artificialLoadInfo and numOfLayers and shall follow the normal procedure defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6874\_replaced([11192598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlypfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The MCS index shall be interpreted without 256QAM, see **5G\_UP\_ALG\_260\_replaced([11096385](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmv_s_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** for details.
* Structure streamConfig for PDSCH for both CPRI and eCPRI:
* For artificial PDSCH load for DL performance testing:
* numStreamIndex: set according to rank: set to 2 for rank 1/2, set to 4 for rank 3/4.
* streamIndex: (0,1) or (0,1,2,3) if numStreamIndex is 2 or 4 respectively.
* When supercell mode is enabled (numOfSuperSubcells >= 2) the patternId is set to value of 0.
* [CB008577-D ]For FDD Beamforming (NRCELL/actBeamforming = True and NRCELL.cellTechnology is equal to 'FDD'), numStreamIndex , streamIndex and other Precoding related parameters see: [12705556: DL precoding for FDD BF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5zH-4GFAEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) [End CB008577-D]
* For DL artificial load generation over sector beam and for DL artificial load generation for EMF validation, see: 5G\_L2\_18078\_replaced([11150090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Z8ufvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

## 2.13.3 DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation

### 2.13.3.0-2 DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation Feature purpose (ID: 11212247)

**2.13.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11212251`)

DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation
The purpose of the feature is to maximize user’s DL MAC throughput artificially by ensuring its cell-specific buffer status is always above a configurable minimum value. It supplements buffer status handling described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4561\_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). UE(s) and cell(s) are selectable.

---

### 2.13.3.0-3 DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation Activation and deactivation of dummy load generation (ID: 11212258)

**2.13.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11212264`)

DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation
The online modifiable parameter rdEnableDummyLoadDl allows activation/deactivation of the functionality.

---

### 2.13.3.0-4 DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation UE selection for dummy load generation (ID: 11212269)

**2.13.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11212274`)

DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation
When rdEnableDummyLoadDl is set to true, the R&D parameter rdDummyLoadDlLcrIdAndRnti (5G\_L2\_12666\_replaced([11189582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28QiAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) selects the lcrId and the C-RNTI for the dummy-load generation.

If the lcrId is set to 0xFFFF, then all cells are selected.

If the C-RNTI is set to 0xFFFF, then all UEs are selected.

Some notes:

For CA user(s), even if lcrId = 0xFFFF to achieve high throughput in all aggregated and activated cells it requires L2-HI to at least initiate data transmission over Scells (otherwise there might be no Scell traffic).

If C-RNTI != 0xFFFF and lcrId = 0xFFFF then multiple non-CA users of different cells with same C-RNTI might be selected.

User selection can be done before user is set up.

---

### 2.13.3.0-5 DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation Raise L2-LO's DL buffer status to configured minimum (ID: 11212281)

**2.13.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11212286`)

DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation
When a new buffer status for a DRB is received via LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd from L2-LO, L2-PS will check whether this is a UE configured for the dummy-load generation, see 5G\_L2\_12659\_replaced([11212269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-kPGPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If that is the case, L2-PS will override the received buffer status with the configured rdDummyLoadDlBsr if that is larger than the received buffer status.

If it is not larger, the received buffer status will be used instead.

SRBs are excluded from this.

See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4561\_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for legacy handling.

---

### 2.13.3.0-6 DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation Ensure minimum DL buffer status after scheduling (ID: 11212291)

**2.13.3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11212297`)

DL MAC-layer dummy-load generation
After giving an allocation to this UE, the stored buffer status will not be decreased below the configured rdDummyLoadDlBsr.

If the stored buffer status is larger than rdDummyLoadDlBsr, it will be decreased at most up to this value, but not below it.

See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4561\_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for legacy handling.

---

## 2.13.4 Assert verification

### 2.13.4.0-1 Assert verification ET level verification (ID: 11212308)

**2.13.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11212313`)

Assert verification
To verify whether assets are called correctly ET must use rdTriggerFaultL2Ps (5G\_L2\_18940\_replaced([11189609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28RJAfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to trigger it.

During the cell setup, when rdTriggerFaultL2Ps is set to 'true', assert  with proper information will occur - this is an abnormal scenario and should be used only for the verification.

When rdTriggerFaultL2Ps is set to 'false' code is acting in a normal way.

---
